         唤起搜索
        </span>
      </div>

      {/* 搜索框 + 排序 */}
      <div className="flex gap-3">
        <div className="relative flex-1">
          <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground pointer-events-none" />
          <Input
            ref={inputRef}
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
            onFocus={() => setShowHistory(true)}
            placeholder="搜索 GitHub…"
            className="pl-9 bg-secondary border-border text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground text-base"
          />
          {/* 搜索历史下拉 */}
          {showHistory && history.length > 0 && (
            <div
              ref={historyRef}
              className="absolute top-full left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-popover border border-border rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50 overflow-hidden"
            >
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 border-b border-border">
                <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium flex items-center gap-1.5">
                  <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />搜索历史
                </span>
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={handleClearHistory}
                  className="text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive transition-colors"
                >
                  清除全部
                </button>
              </div>
              <div className="max-h-48 overflow-y-auto">
                {history.map((item, idx) => (
                  <button
                    key={idx}
                    type="button"
                    className="w-full flex items-center gap-2.5 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-foreground hover:bg-secondary/60 transition-colors text-left"
                    onMouseDown={(e) => {
                      // 防止 blur 先触发隐藏历史
                      e.preventDefault();
                      setQuery(item);
                      handleSearch(item, searchType, 1);
                    }}
                  >
                    <Clock className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
                    <span className="flex-1 truncate">{item}</span>
                    <X
                      className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground shrink-0"
                      onClick={(e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        const next = history.filter((_, i) => i !== idx);
                        localStorage.setItem(HISTORY_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(next));
                        setHistory(next);
                      }}
                    />
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 排序下拉（仅仓库搜索有效） */}
        {searchType === 'repositories' && (
          <DropdownMenu>
            <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
              <Button
                variant="outline"
                size="sm"
                className="shrink-0 h-9 gap-1.5 border-border bg-secondary text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80 text-xs hidden sm:flex"
              >
                <ArrowUpDown className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                {currentSortLabel}
              </Button>
            </DropdownMenuTrigger>
            <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="bg-popover border-border w-40">
              <DropdownMenuLabel className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">排序方式</DropdownMenuLabel>
              <DropdownMenuSeparator className="bg-border" />
              {SORT_OPTIONS.map(opt => (
                <DropdownMenuItem
                  key={opt.value}
                  className={cn(
                    'cursor-pointer text-sm',
                    sortOption === opt.value ? 'text-primary font-medium' : 'text-foreground'
                  )}
                  onClick={() => handleSortChange(opt.value)}
                >
                  {opt.label}
                  {sortOption === opt.value && <span className="ml-auto text-primary text-xs">✓</span>}
                </DropdownMenuItem>
              ))}
            </DropdownMenuContent>
          </DropdownMenu>
        )}

        <Button
          className="bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90 shrink-0"
          onClick={() => handleSearch(query, searchType, 1)}
          disabled={loading || !query.trim()}
        >
          搜索
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* 搜索类型选项卡 */}

   568     /**
   569      * DownloadListener：拦截 WebView 触发的下载。
   570      *
   571      * 两种场景：
   572      * 1. blob: URL（安全网）——前端通常已通过 AndroidBridge 处理，此处作为兜底。
   573      * 2. https: URL——从 localStorage 读取 token，走"解析重定向 → DownloadManager"流程。
   574      */
   575     private fun setupDownloadListener() {
   576         webView.setDownloadListener { url, _, contentDisposition, mimetype, _ ->
   577             val fileName = URLUtil.guessFileName(url, contentDisposition, mimetype)
   578 
   579             if (url.startsWith("blob:")) {
   580                 // blob: URL 安全网：通过 JS 读内容再传给 saveBlobData
   581                 val safeUrl = url.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
   582                 val safeName = fileName.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
   583                 val safeMime = mimetype.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
   584                 val js = """
   585                     (function(){
   586                         fetch('$safeUrl')
   587                             .then(function(r){return r.blob();})
   588                             .then(function(blob){
   589                                 var reader=new FileReader();
   590                                 reader.onloadend=function(){
   591                                     var b64=(reader.result||'').toString().split(',')[1]||'';
   592                                     window.AndroidBridge&&window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData('$safeName','$safeMime',b64);
   593                                 };
   594                                 reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
   595                             })
   596                             .catch(function(e){
   597                                 console.warn('[AndroidDownload] blob fetch failed:',e.message);
   598                                 window.AndroidBridge&&window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData('$safeName','','');
   599                             });
   600                     })()
   601                 """.trimIndent()
   602                 webView.evaluateJavascript(js, null)
   603                 return@setDownloadListener
   604             }
   605 
   606             // https: URL：读取 token 后解析重定向再下载
   607             webView.evaluateJavascript(
   608                 "(function(){ try { return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_token') || '' } catch(e){ return '' } })()"
   609             ) { result ->
   610                 val token = result?.removeSurrounding("\"")?.trim() ?: ""
   611                 checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
   612             }
   613         }
   614     }

   146         /**
   147          * ArtifactsPage 调用：传原始 GitHub URL + token，由原生完成"解析重定向 → 下载"流程。
   148          *
   149          * GitHub 所有下载链接（releases/archive/artifacts）均会 302 重定向到
   150          * S3/CDN 预签名 URL。直接把 Authorization header 转发给预签名 URL 会
   151          * 触发 S3 签名冲突，导致下载失败。此方法先解析最终 URL 再下载，避免此问题。

   153          * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.downloadFile(url, fileName, token)

   166          * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData(fileName, mimeType, base64Content)

   169         @JavascriptInterface

   385             /**
   386              * 每次页面导航完成后，从 URL fragment（HashRouter）中解析当前路径，
   387              * 并同步更新底部导航栏的选中状态。
   388              * 例如：file:///android_asset/index.html#/repos/owner/name → path = "/repos/..."
   389              */
   390             override fun onPageFinished(view: WebView?, url: String?) {
   391                 super.onPageFinished(view, url)
   392                 val hash = url?.substringAfter("#", "") ?: return
   393                 val path = if (hash.startsWith("/")) hash else "/$hash"
   394                 syncBottomNavSelection(path)
   395 
   396                 // 首次加载完成后从 localStorage 读取主题并同步原生颜色
   397                 // github_manager_theme 是 ThemeContext 使用的 key
   398                 view?.evaluateJavascript(
   399                     "(function(){ return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_theme') || 'dark'; })()"
   400                 ) { result ->
   401                     val raw = result?.trim('"') ?: "dark"
   402                     val resolved = when (raw) {
   403                         "light" -> false
   404                         "dark"  -> true
   405                         else    -> { // system
   406                             val nightMode = resources.configuration.uiMode and
   407                                 android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_MASK
   408                             nightMode == android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_YES
   409                         }
   410                     }
   411                     runOnUiThread { applyNativeTheme(resolved) }
   412                 }
   413             }
   414         }
   415     }
   416 
   417     /**
   418      * 根据当前路径前缀匹配导航菜单项，并更新 BottomNavigationView 选中状态。
   419      * 采用静默更新方式（禁用监听器 → 修改选中项 → 恢复监听器），避免触发重复导航。
   420      */
   421     private fun syncBottomNavSelection(path: String) {
   422         val targetId = navPathMap.entries.firstOrNull { (prefix, _) ->
   423             if (prefix == "/") path == "/" else path.startsWith(prefix)
   424         }?.value ?: R.id.nav_home
   425 
   426         if (targetId == currentNavItemId) return
   427         currentNavItemId = targetId
   428 
   429         // 静默更新：临时移除监听器，防止 setSelectedItemId 触发重复路由跳转
   430         bottomNav.setOnItemSelectedListener(null)
   431         bottomNav.selectedItemId = targetId
   432         setupBottomNavListener()
   433     }
   434 
   435     /**
   436      * 初始化底部导航栏：绑定点击监听，通过 evaluateJavascript 修改 HashRouter location。
   437      * 仅在目标 Tab 与当前页面不同时才执行导航，避免重刷当前页。
   438      */
   439     private fun setupBottomNav() {
   440         bottomNav.selectedItemId = R.id.nav_home
   441         setupBottomNavListener()
   442     }

    92 interface ThemeContextValue {
    93   theme: ThemeMode;
    94   setTheme: (t: ThemeMode) => void;
    95   resolvedTheme: 'dark' | 'light';
    96   accentSchemeId: string;
    97   setAccentScheme: (id: string) => void;
    98 }
    99 
   100 const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextValue | null>(null);
   101 const STORAGE_KEY        = 'github_manager_theme';
   102 const ACCENT_STORAGE_KEY = 'github_manager_accent';
   103 const DARK_COLOR  = '#1e1b4b';
   104 const LIGHT_COLOR = '#f5f3ff';
   105 
   106 function getSystemTheme(): 'dark' | 'light' {
   107   return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches ? 'dark' : 'light';
   108 }
   109 
   110 /** 同步更新 <meta name="theme-color"> 让安卓 WebView 状态栏颜色与页面一致 */
   111 function updateThemeColorMeta(isDark: boolean) {
   112   const meta = document.querySelector<HTMLMetaElement>('meta[name="theme-color"]:not([media])');
   113   if (meta) meta.setAttribute('content', isDark ? DARK_COLOR : LIGHT_COLOR);
   114 }
   115 
   116 /** 将主题色方案注入 CSS 变量 */
   117 function applyAccentScheme(scheme: AccentScheme, resolved: 'dark' | 'light') {
   118   const root = document.documentElement;
   119   const isDark = resolved === 'dark';
   120   root.style.setProperty('--primary', isDark ? scheme.darkPrimary : scheme.lightPrimary);
   121   root.style.setProperty('--accent',  isDark ? scheme.darkAccent  : scheme.lightAccent);
   122   root.style.setProperty('--ring',    isDark ? scheme.darkRing    : scheme.lightRing);
   123   // sidebar-primary / sidebar-ring 同步
   124   root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-primary', isDark ? scheme.darkPrimary : scheme.lightPrimary);
   125   root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-ring',    isDark ? scheme.darkRing    : scheme.lightRing);
   126 }
   127 
   128 function applyTheme(mode: ThemeMode) {
   129   const resolved = mode === 'system' ? getSystemTheme() : mode;
   130   const html = document.documentElement;
   131   if (resolved === 'dark') {
   132     html.classList.add('dark');
   133     html.classList.remove('light');
   134   } else {
   135     html.classList.add('light');
   136     html.classList.remove('dark');
   137   }
   138   updateThemeColorMeta(resolved === 'dark');
   139   // 通知 APK 壳同步更新状态栏与底部导航栏颜色
   140   notifyAndroidTheme(resolved === 'dark');
   141   return resolved;
   142 }
   143 
   144 /**
   145  * 向 Android 原生层推送主题变化。
   146  * AndroidBridge 由 MainActivity 的 addJavascriptInterface 注入，
   147  * 纯浏览器环境中不存在，通过可选链安全调用。
   148  */
   149 function notifyAndroidTheme(isDark: boolean) {
   150   try {
   151     (window as unknown as { AndroidBridge?: { notifyTheme?: (d: boolean) => void } })
   152       .AndroidBridge?.notifyTheme?.(isDark);
   153   } catch {
   154     // 非 APK 环境或旧版本壳，静默忽略
   155   }
   156 }
   157 
   158 /**
   159  * 触发主题切换过渡动画：
   160  * 向 <html> 添加 theme-transitioning class，CSS 中借助它激活全局 transition，
   161  * 动画结束后移除，避免页面初始加载时也触发不必要的过渡。
   162  */
   163 function triggerThemeTransition(callback: () => void) {
   164   const html = document.documentElement;
   165   html.classList.add('theme-transitioning');
   166   callback();
   167   // 等待最长过渡时长后移除（300ms 与 CSS 对齐）
   168   setTimeout(() => html.classList.remove('theme-transitioning'), 350);
   169 }
   170 
   171 export function ThemeProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
   172   const [theme, setThemeState] = useState<ThemeMode>(() => {
   173     const saved = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) as ThemeMode | null;
   174     return saved || 'dark';
   175   });
   176   const [resolvedTheme, setResolvedTheme] = useState<'dark' | 'light'>(() =>
   177     applyTheme((localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) as ThemeMode | null) || 'dark')
   178   );
   179 
   180   // ── 主题色方案 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   181   const [accentSchemeId, setAccentSchemeIdState] = useState<string>(() => {
   182     return localStorage.getItem(ACCENT_STORAGE_KEY) || 'purple';
   183   });
   184 
   185   // 初始化时立即应用已保存的色方案
   186   useEffect(() => {
   187     const scheme = ACCENT_SCHEMES.find(s => s.id === accentSchemeId) ?? ACCENT_SCHEMES[0];
   188     applyAccentScheme(scheme, resolvedTheme);
   189   // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
   190   }, []);
   191 
   192   const setAccentScheme = useCallback((id: string) => {
   193     const scheme = ACCENT_SCHEMES.find(s => s.id === id) ?? ACCENT_SCHEMES[0];
   194     localStorage.setItem(ACCENT_STORAGE_KEY, scheme.id);
   195     setAccentSchemeIdState(scheme.id);
   196     applyAccentScheme(scheme, resolvedTheme);
   197   }, [resolvedTheme]);
   198 
   199   const setTheme = useCallback((t: ThemeMode) => {
   200     localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, t);
   201     setThemeState(t);
   202     triggerThemeTransition(() => {
   203       const resolved = applyTheme(t);
   204       setResolvedTheme(resolved);
   205       // 切换明暗时重新应用当前色方案，确保色值对应正确的明暗变体
   206       const savedId = localStorage.getItem(ACCENT_STORAGE_KEY) || 'purple';
   207       const scheme = ACCENT_SCHEMES.find(s => s.id === savedId) ?? ACCENT_SCHEMES[0];
   208       applyAccentScheme(scheme, resolved);
   209     });
   210   }, []);
   211 
   212   // 跟随系统变化
   213   useEffect(() => {
   214     if (theme !== 'system') return;
   215     const mq = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
   216     const handler = () => {
   217       triggerThemeTransition(() => {
   218         const resolved = applyTheme('system');
   219         setResolvedTheme(resolved);
   220         const savedId = localStorage.getItem(ACCENT_STORAGE_KEY) || 'purple';
   221         const scheme = ACCENT_SCHEMES.find(s => s.id === savedId) ?? ACCENT_SCHEMES[0];
   222         applyAccentScheme(scheme, resolved);
   223       });
   224     };
   225     mq.addEventListener('change', handler);
   226     return () => mq.removeEventListener('change', handler);
   227   }, [theme]);
   228 
   229   return (
   230     <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, setTheme, resolvedTheme, accentSchemeId, setAccentScheme }}>
   231       {children}
   232     </ThemeContext.Provider>
   233   );
   234 }
   235 
   236 export function useTheme(): ThemeContextValue {
   237   const ctx = useContext(ThemeContext);
   238   if (!ctx) throw new Error('useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider');
   239   return ctx;
   240 }

   474             key={type}
   475             type="button"
   476             className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2.5 text-sm border-b-2 transition-colors ${
   477               searchType === type
   478                 ? 'border-primary text-foreground font-medium'
   479                 : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
   480             }`}
   481             onClick={() => {
   482               setSearchType(type);
   483               setCurrentPage(1);
   484               if (query.trim()) handleSearch(query, type, 1);
   485             }}
   486           >
   487             <Icon className="w-4 h-4" />
   488             {label}
   489           </button>
   490         ))}
   491       </div>
   492 
   493       {/* 结果数量 + 移动端排序 */}

```
New String: ```
  // 关闭操作：非编辑模式直接清理；编辑模式返回上级目录
  // replace=true 时用 replace 导航，避免关闭后按返回键重新打开编辑器
  const closeAction = (returnToParent = false) => {
    setActionMode(null);
    setActionTarget(null);
    setCommitMsg('');
    setNewFileName('');
    setNewFileContent('');
    setNewFolderName('');
    setRenameTo('');
    setMoveTo('');
    setDeleteProgress(null);
    setEditorFullscreen(false);
    setShowSearch(false);
    setSearchQuery('');
    setSearchMatchIndex(0);
    if (returnToParent && filePath) {
      const parentParts = filePath.split('/').slice(0, -1);
      // replace: true 将当前文件路由条目替换为父目录，而非新增入栈，
      // 这样用户按返回键时不会重新打开编辑器
      navigate(
        `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/code${parentParts.length ? '/' + parentParts.join('/') : ''}`,
        { replace: true }
      );
    }
  };
```

/** 将主题色方案注入 CSS 变量 */
function applyAccentScheme(scheme: AccentScheme, resolved: 'dark' | 'light') {
  const root = document.documentElement;
  const isDark = resolved === 'dark';
  root.style.setProperty('--primary', isDark ? scheme.darkPrimary : scheme.lightPrimary);
  root.style.setProperty('--accent',  isDark ? scheme.darkAccent  : scheme.lightAccent);
  root.style.setProperty('--ring',    isDark ? scheme.darkRing    : scheme.lightRing);
  // sidebar-primary / sidebar-ring 同步
  root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-primary', isDark ? scheme.darkPrimary : scheme.lightPrimary);
  root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-ring',    isDark ? scheme.darkRing    : scheme.lightRing);
}
```
New String: ```
/** 将主题色方案注入 CSS 变量，并同步通知 Android 底部导航栏选中色 */
function applyAccentScheme(scheme: AccentScheme, resolved: 'dark' | 'light') {
  const root = document.documentElement;
  const isDark = resolved === 'dark';
  root.style.setProperty('--primary', isDark ? scheme.darkPrimary : scheme.lightPrimary);
  root.style.setProperty('--accent',  isDark ? scheme.darkAccent  : scheme.lightAccent);
  root.style.setProperty('--ring',    isDark ? scheme.darkRing    : scheme.lightRing);
  // sidebar-primary / sidebar-ring 同步
  root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-primary', isDark ? scheme.darkPrimary : scheme.lightPrimary);
  root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-ring',    isDark ? scheme.darkRing    : scheme.lightRing);
  // 通知 Android 原生底部导航栏选中色跟随方案
  notifyAndroidAccent(scheme.previewColor);
}

New String: ```
/**
 * 向 Android 原生层推送主题变化。
 * AndroidBridge 由 MainActivity 的 addJavascriptInterface 注入，
 * 纯浏览器环境中不存在，通过可选链安全调用。
 */
function notifyAndroidTheme(isDark: boolean) {
  try {
    (window as unknown as { AndroidBridge?: { notifyTheme?: (d: boolean) => void } })
      .AndroidBridge?.notifyTheme?.(isDark);
  } catch {
    // 非 APK 环境或旧版本壳，静默忽略
  }
}

/**
 * 向 Android 原生层推送强调色变化，使底部导航栏选中色同步跟随。
 * @param primaryHex 当前方案的预览 hex 色值，如 "#7c3aed"
 */
function notifyAndroidAccent(primaryHex: string) {
  try {
    (window as unknown as { AndroidBridge?: { notifyAccent?: (hex: string) => void } })
      .AndroidBridge?.notifyAccent?.(primaryHex);
  } catch {
    // 非 APK 环境或旧版本壳，静默忽略

Command: str_replace
Old String: ```

```
New String: ```
        /**
         * 主题切换时由 ThemeContext 调用，同步更新原生状态栏与底部导航栏外观。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.notifyTheme(isDark: boolean)
         * @param isDark true = 深色主题，false = 浅色主题
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyTheme(isDark: Boolean) {
            runOnUiThread { applyNativeTheme(isDark) }
        }

        /**
         * 强调色方案切换时由 ThemeContext 调用，同步更新底部导航栏选中图标/文字颜色。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.notifyAccent(primaryHex: string)
         * @param primaryHex 当前方案的主色调 hex 值，如 "#7c3aed"
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyAccent(primaryHex: String) {
            runOnUiThread {
                try {
                    val color = Color.parseColor(primaryHex)
                    // 仅更新选中色，未选中色保持不变（取自当前 itemTextColor/iconTintList）
                    val unselected = if (isDarkTheme()) 0xFF9292A8.toInt() else 0xFF64748B.toInt()
                    val iconColors = android.content.res.ColorStateList(
                        arrayOf(intArrayOf(android.R.attr.state_checked), intArrayOf()),
                        intArrayOf(color, unselected)
                    )
                    bottomNav.itemIconTintList = iconColors
                    bottomNav.itemTextColor   = iconColors
                    currentAccentColor = color
                } catch (_: Exception) { /* 非法 hex，静默忽略 */ }
            }
        }
```

    74                         Array(data.clipData!!.itemCount) { i ->
    75                             data.clipData!!.getItemAt(i).uri
    76                         }
    77                     data.data != null -> arrayOf(data.data!!)
    78                     else -> cameraImageUri?.let { arrayOf(it) }
    79                 }
    80             }
    81         } else null
    82         fileChooserCallback?.onReceiveValue(uris)
    83         fileChooserCallback = null
    84     }

    private fun applyNativeTheme(isDark: Boolean) {

                // 首次加载完成后从 localStorage 读取主题并同步原生颜色
                // github_manager_theme 是 ThemeContext 使用的 key
                view?.evaluateJavascript(
                    "(function(){ return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_theme') || 'dark'; })()"
                ) { result ->
                    val raw = result?.trim('"') ?: "dark"
                    val resolved = when (raw) {
                        "light" -> false
                        "dark"  -> true
                        else    -> { // system
                            val nightMode = resources.configuration.uiMode and
                                android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_MASK
                            nightMode == android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_YES
                        }
                    }
                    runOnUiThread { applyNativeTheme(resolved) }

                    // 同时读取强调色方案，将选中色同步为存储的 previewColor

                        "orange" to "#f97316",
                        "rose"   to "#e11d48",

  const handleSortChange = (newSort: SortOption) => {
    localStorage.setItem(SORT_STORAGE_KEY, newSort);
    setSortOption(newSort);
    if (searched && query.trim()) {
      handleSearch(query, searchType, 1, newSort);
    }
  };

  // 点击搜索框左侧图标：循环切换排序方式（仅仓库搜索时有效）
  const cycleSortOption = () => {
    if (searchType !== 'repositories') return;
    const idx = SORT_OPTIONS.findIndex(o => o.value === sortOption);
    const next = SORT_OPTIONS[(idx + 1) % SORT_OPTIONS.length];
    handleSortChange(next.value);
  };

          {/* 左侧图标：仓库搜索时为可点击的排序图标（下拉选择），其他类型为静态搜索图标 */}
          {searchType === 'repositories' ? (() => {

            return (
              <DropdownMenu>
                <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
                  <button

The `include` tag can have an ID that overrides the root element\'s ID. But actually `<include>` with an ID sets the ID on the included root view. So as long as splash_screen.xml has a root with some ID (or no ID), the `include`\'s `android:id` will override it. Let me verify: yes, if `<include android:id="@+id/splashOverlay">` the root view of the included layout gets that ID.\n\nSo plan:\n- `splash_screen.xml` root = FrameLayout (no android:id, or any id)\n- In `activity_main.xml`: `<include layout="@layout/splash_screen" android:id="@+id/splashOverlay" ... />`\n\nFor the decorative grid dots / lines, I can:\n- Use multiple thin View strips with low opacity\n- Create a dots pattern using a shape with dashed stroke\n\nLet me design the layout now:\n\n```xml\n<!-- splash_screen.xml - New String: ```
    private fun dismissSplash() {
        if (splashDismissed) return
        splashDismissed = true
        // 淡出 + 轻微缩小，营造优雅的启动画面消散效果
        splashOverlay.animate()
            .alpha(0f)
            .scaleX(1.04f)
            .scaleY(1.04f)
            .setDuration(380)
            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }
            .start()
    }

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nAndroid\'s standard approach for dark/light mode theming is to use:\n1. `res/values/` for light mode colors\n2. `res/values-night/` for dark mode colors\n\nThen in the layout/drawables, reference color resources like `@color/splash_bg` which automatically resolves to the correct value based on the current system mode.\n\nCurrent splash has hardcoded hex colors everywhere. The plan:\n\n1. Add splash color tokens to `res/values/colors.xml` (light mode values)\n2. Create `res/values-night/colors.xml` with dark mode values for the same tokens\n3. Update `splash_background.xml`, `splash_logo_bg.xml`, `splash_divider.xml` to use `@color/` references\n4. Update `splash_screen.xml` to use `@color/` references for all hardcoded colors\n\n**Light mode palette** (clean, professional, GitHub-light inspired):\n- splash_bg: #F6F8FA (GitHub light background)\n- splash_bg_gradient_end: #EAEEF2\n- splash_glow: subtle purple tint, low opacity\n- splash_logo_outer_glow: #15A855F5 (light purple tint)\n- splash_logo_mid_glow: #25A855F5\n- splash_logo_circle_start: #EDE7FF (light lavender)\n- splash_logo_circle_end: #D8CCF8\n- splash_logo_stroke: #9B6EF8\n- splash_logo_icon_tint: #7C3AED (dark purple for contrast on light bg)\n- splash_title: #1F2328 (dark text)\n- splash_subtitle: #656D76\n- splash_divider_mid: #7C3AED with 60% opacity\n- splash_prompt: #7C3AED\n- splash_terminal_text: #8C959F\n- splash_cursor: #7C3AED\n- splash_corner_line: #407C3AED\n- splash_progress_tint: #7C3AED\n- splash_loading_text: #8C959F\n\n**Dark mode palette** (current design, geek terminal):\n- splash_bg: #08080E\n- splash_logo_outer_glow: #158B4CF8\n- splash_logo_mid_glow: #258B4CF8\n- splash_logo_circle_start: #3D1A7A\n- splash_logo_circle_end: #1A0840\n- splash_logo_stroke: #7C4CF0\n- splash_logo_icon_tint: #FFFFFF\n- splash_title: #F0F6FF\n- splash_subtitle: #8B949E\n- splash_prompt: #7C4CF0\n- splash_terminal_text: #484F58\n- splash_cursor: #7C4CF0\n- splash_corner_line: #407C4CF0\n- splash_progress_tint: #8B4CF8\n- splash_loading_text: #484F58\n\nNow the issue is that XML drawables (splash_background.xml, splash_logo_bg.xml, splash_divider.xml) use hardcoded colors. Android supports `@color/` references in drawables, and those resolve correctly based on the current configuration (night mode or not). So I can use `@color/` references there too.\n\nLet me also note: `android:tint` in ImageView can use `@color/` reference, and `android:background` on Views can use `@color/` reference.\n\nHowever, for `android:indeterminateTint` and `android:progressTint`, those need a `@color/` reference to work properly with themes.\n\nOne complexity: the gradient drawables in splash_background.xml use `android:startColor` and `android:endColor` which CAN reference `@color/` values. Let me verify - yes, in Android XML drawables you can use `@color/` references in gradient attributes.\n\nLet me plan all the color tokens needed:\n\n**Drawable tokens:**\n- `splash_bg_base` - base solid background color\n- `splash_glow_start` - radial glow center color (with alpha)\n- `splash_logo_outer` - logo outermost glow  \n- `splash_logo_mid` - logo middle glow\n- `splash_logo_inner_start` - logo circle gradient start\n- `splash_logo_inner_end` - logo circle gradient end\n- `splash_logo_stroke` - logo circle border\n- `splash_divider_color` - center color of divider line\n\n**Layout tokens:**\n- `splash_corner_line` - corner decoration lines\n- `splash_icon_tint` - Octocat icon tint\n- `splash_title_text` - app name\n- `splash_subtitle_text` - tagline\n- `splash_prompt_color` - terminal $ prompt + cursor\n- `splash_terminal_text` - terminal command text\n- `splash_progress_tint` - progress bar\n- `splash_loading_text` - "正在启动…"\n\nThis is a clean approach. Let me implement it.\n\nNote: For gradient drawables, `@color/` with alpha embedded in the color (like `#158B4CF8`) can\'t be split easily. I\'ll define the full ARGB colors directly in colors.xml.\n\nActually I realize I should be careful: in `splash_background.xml`, the radial glow uses `android:startColor="#1A0A2E"` and `android:endColor="#0008080E"` - these have alpha embedded.    131     // ── JS 桥接口 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   132     inner class WebAppBridge {
   133 
   134         /** React 首屏就绪后调用，触发启动遮罩淡出 */
   135         @JavascriptInterface
   136         fun notifyReady() {
   137             runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
   138         }
   139 
   140         /**
   141          * 主题切换时由 ThemeContext 调用，同步更新原生状态栏与底部导航栏外观。
   142          *
   143          * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.notifyTheme(isDark: boolean)
   144          * @param isDark true = 深色主题，false = 浅色主题
   145          */
   146         @JavascriptInterface
   147         fun notifyTheme(isDark: Boolean) {
   148             runOnUiThread { applyNativeTheme(isDark) }
   149         }
   150 
   151         /**
   152          * 强调色方案切换时由 ThemeContext 调用，同步更新底部导航栏选中图标/文字颜色。
   153          *
   154          * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.notifyAccent(primaryHex: string)
   155          * @param primaryHex 当前方案的主色调 hex 值，如 "#7c3aed"
   156          */
   157         @JavascriptInterface
   158         fun notifyAccent(primaryHex: String) {
   159             runOnUiThread {
   160                 try {
   161                     val color = Color.parseColor(primaryHex)
   162                     // 仅更新选中色，未选中色保持不变（取自当前 itemTextColor/iconTintList）
   163                     val unselected = if (isDarkTheme()) 0xFF9292A8.toInt() else 0xFF64748B.toInt()
   164                     val iconColors = android.content.res.ColorStateList(
   165                         arrayOf(intArrayOf(android.R.attr.state_checked), intArrayOf()),
   166                         intArrayOf(color, unselected)
   167                     )
   168                     bottomNav.itemIconTintList = iconColors
   169                     bottomNav.itemTextColor   = iconColors
   170                     currentAccentColor = color
   171                 } catch (_: Exception) { /* 非法 hex，静默忽略 */ }
   172             }
   173         }
   174 
   175         /**
   176          * ArtifactsPage 调用：传原始 GitHub URL + token，由原生完成"解析重定向 → 下载"流程。
   177          *
   178          * GitHub 所有下载链接（releases/archive/artifacts）均会 302 重定向到
   179          * S3/CDN 预签名 URL。直接把 Authorization header 转发给预签名 URL 会
   180          * 触发 S3 签名冲突，导致下载失败。此方法先解析最终 URL 再下载，避免此问题。
   181          *
   182          * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.downloadFile(url, fileName, token)
   183          */
   184         @JavascriptInterface
   185         fun downloadFile(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
   186             runOnUiThread {
   187                 checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
   188             }
   189         }
   190 
   191         /**
   192          * ExportPage 调用：传内存文本内容（Base64 编码），由原生写入「下载」文件夹。
   193          * 适用于 JSON/CSV 导出等纯文本内容，不经过 DownloadManager。
   194          *
   195          * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData(fileName, mimeType, base64Content)
   196          * 此方法运行在 JavascriptInterface 后台线程。
   197          */
   198         @JavascriptInterface
   199         fun saveBlobData(fileName: String, mimeType: String, base64Content: String) {
   200             if (base64Content.isEmpty()) {
   201                 runOnUiThread {
   202                     Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "保存失败：内容为空", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
   203                 }
   204                 return
   205             }
   206             if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT < Build.VERSION_CODES.Q) {
   207                 val granted = checkSelfPermission(Manifest.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE) ==
   208                     PackageManager.PERMISSION_GRANTED
   209                 if (!granted) {
   210                     runOnUiThread {
   211                         Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "请授予存储权限后重试", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
   212                     }
   213                     return
   214                 }
   215             }

   295         val hex = getSharedPreferences("gm_prefs", MODE_PRIVATE)
   296             .getString("accent_hex", "#8B4CF8") ?: "#8B4CF8"

   335                     }
   336                 }
   337             }
   338         } catch (_: Exception) { /* 非法 hex，使用 XML 默认色，静默忽略 */ }

   389     @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
   390     override fun onBackPressed() {
   391         // 通过 JS history.back() 触发 HashRouter popstate，
   392         // 避免 webView.goBack() 重新加载整个 HTML 页面。
   393         // React Router v6 在 history.state.idx 中记录当前历史栈深度：
   394         //   idx > 0  → 有可返回的路由历史，调用 JS history.back()
   395         //   idx == 0 → 已在根页面，进入双击退出逻辑
   396         webView.evaluateJavascript(
   397             "(function(){ var s=window.history.state; return (s&&s.idx>0)?'1':'0'; })()"
   398         ) { result ->
   399             runOnUiThread {
   400                 if (result?.trim('"') == "1") {
   401                     // 有路由历史：让 React Router 处理返回，页面不重载
   402                     webView.evaluateJavascript("window.history.back()", null)
   403                 } else {
   404                     // 已在根页面：双击退出
   405                     handleExitOnBack()
   406                 }
   407             }
   408         }
   409     }
   410 
   411     /** 双击退出逻辑：2 秒内连按两次返回键才退出，避免误触。 */
   412     private var backPressedOnce = false
   413     private val backHandler = Handler(Looper.getMainLooper())
   414 
   415     private fun handleExitOnBack() {
   416         if (backPressedOnce) {
   417             // 第二次按下：退出应用
   418             backHandler.removeCallbacksAndMessages(null)
   419             finish()
   420             return
   421         }
   422         backPressedOnce = true
   423         Toast.makeText(this, "再按一次退出应用", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
   424         // 2 秒后重置标志
   425         backHandler.postDelayed({ backPressedOnce = false }, 2000)
   426     }

   453     private fun setupWebViewClient() {
   454         webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
   455             override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
   456                 view: WebView?,
   457                 request: WebResourceRequest?,
   458             ): Boolean {
   459                 val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
   460 
   461                 // 本地资源：让 WebView 自己处理
   462                 if (url.startsWith("file://")) return false
   463 
   464                 // 外部链接（http/https）：一律用系统浏览器打开，避免破坏 React 应用历史栈。
   465                 // 若允许 WebView 加载外部页面，React Router 的 history.state.idx
   466                 // 会丢失，返回键无法回到应用内部路由。
   467                 if (url.startsWith("https://") || url.startsWith("http://")) {
   468                     runCatching {
   469                         val intent = Intent(Intent.ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(url))
   470                         startActivity(intent)
   471                     }
   472                     return true // 阻止 WebView 自行加载
   473                 }
   474 
   475                 // 其他协议（tel:、mailto: 等）：交系统处理
   476                 return true
   477             }
   478 
   479             /**
   480              * 每次页面导航完成后，从 URL fragment（HashRouter）中解析当前路径，
   481              * 并同步更新底部导航栏的选中状态。
   482              * 例如：file:///android_asset/index.html#/repos/owner/name → path = "/repos/..."
   483              */
   484             override fun onPageFinished(view: WebView?, url: String?) {
   485                 super.onPageFinished(view, url)
   486                 val hash = url?.substringAfter("#", "") ?: return
   487                 val path = if (hash.startsWith("/")) hash else "/$hash"

   504                     }

   510                         "blue"   to "#1d6be3",

   541     /**
   542      * 根据当前路径前缀匹配导航菜单项，并更新 BottomNavigationView 选中状态。
   543      * 采用静默更新方式（禁用监听器 → 修改选中项 → 恢复监听器），避免触发重复导航。
   544      */
   545     private fun syncBottomNavSelection(path: String) {
   546         val targetId = navPathMap.entries.firstOrNull { (prefix, _) ->
   547             if (prefix == "/") path == "/" else path.startsWith(prefix)
   548         }?.value ?: R.id.nav_home
   549 
   550         if (targetId == currentNavItemId) return
   551         currentNavItemId = targetId

   554         bottomNav.setOnItemSelectedListener(null)
   555         bottomNav.selectedItemId = targetId
   556         setupBottomNavListener()
